   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    National Recording Registry
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
     <span class="mw-redirectedfrom">
      (Redirected from
      <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_recordings_preserved_in_the_United_States_National_Recording_Registry&amp;redirect=no" title="List of recordings preserved in the United States National Recording Registry">
       List of recordings preserved in the United States National Recording Registry
      </a>
      )
     </span>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1403" data-file-width="1296" height="238" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg/220px-Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg/330px-Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg/440px-Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Martin_Luther_King_-_March_on_Washington.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Martin_Luther_King_Jr." title="Martin Luther King Jr.">
         Martin Luther King Jr.
        </a>
        's "
        <a href="/wiki/I_Have_a_Dream" title="I Have a Dream">
         I Have a Dream
        </a>
        " speech was one of the 50 recordings added on the first year of existence of the United States National Recording Registry.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      The
      <b>
       National Recording Registry
      </b>
      is a list of sound recordings that "are culturally, historically, or aesthetically important, and/or inform or reflect life in the United States." The registry was established by the National Recording Preservation Act of 2000,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRPB_1-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRPB-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      which created the
      <a href="/wiki/National_Recording_Preservation_Board" title="National Recording Preservation Board">
       National Recording Preservation Board
      </a>
      , whose members are appointed by the
      <a href="/wiki/Librarian_of_Congress" title="Librarian of Congress">
       Librarian of Congress
      </a>
      . The recordings preserved in the United States National Recording Registry form a registry of
      <a href="/wiki/Recording" title="Recording">
       recordings
      </a>
      selected yearly by the
      <a href="/wiki/National_Recording_Preservation_Board" title="National Recording Preservation Board">
       National Recording Preservation Board
      </a>
      for preservation in the
      <a href="/wiki/Library_of_Congress" title="Library of Congress">
       Library of Congress
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CR_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-CR-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The legislative intent of the National Recording Preservation Act of 2000 was to develop a national program to guard America's
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sound_recording" title="Sound recording">
       sound recording
      </a>
      heritage. The Act resulted in the formations of the National Recording Registry, The National Recording Preservation Board and a fund-raising foundation to aid their efforts.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-O_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-O-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The act established the Registry specifically for the purpose of maintaining and preserving sound recordings and collections of sound recordings that are culturally, historically, or aesthetically significant.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRPB_1-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRPB-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Beginning in 2002, the National Recording Preservation Board began selecting nominated recordings each year to be preserved.
     </p>
     <p>
      The first four yearly lists included 50 selections. However, since 2006, 25 recordings have been selected annually. Thus, a total of 425 recordings have been preserved in the Registry as of 2014
      <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">
       <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit">
        [update]
       </a>
      </sup>
      . Each calendar year, public nominations are accepted for inclusion in that year's list of selections to be announced the following spring. Nominations are made in the following categories:
     </p>
     <div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
      <ul>
       <li>
        Blues
       </li>
       <li>
        Broadway/Musical Theatre/Soundtrack
       </li>
       <li>
        Cajun/Zydeco/"Swamp"
       </li>
       <li>
        Children's recordings
       </li>
       <li>
        Choral
       </li>
       <li>
        Classical
       </li>
       <li>
        Comedy/Novelty
       </li>
       <li>
        Country/Bluegrass
       </li>
       <li>
        Documentary/Broadcast/Spoken Word
       </li>
       <li>
        Environmental
       </li>
       <li>
        Field
       </li>
       <li>
        Folk/Ethnic
       </li>
       <li>
        Gospel/Spiritual
       </li>
       <li>
        Heavy Metal
       </li>
       <li>
        Jazz
       </li>
       <li>
        Latin
       </li>
       <li>
        Pop (pre-1955)
       </li>
       <li>
        Pop (post-1955)
       </li>
       <li>
        R&amp;B
       </li>
       <li>
        Radio
       </li>
       <li>
        Rap/Hip-hop
       </li>
       <li>
        Rock
       </li>
       <li>
        Technology
       </li>
      </ul>
     </div>
     <p>
      Each yearly list has often included a few recordings that have also been selected for inclusion in the holdings of the
      <a href="/wiki/National_Archives_and_Records_Administration" title="National Archives and Records Administration">
       National Archives
      </a>
      ' audiovisual collection. Those recordings on the Library of Congress' National Recording Registry that are of a political nature will tend to overlap with the audiovisual collection of the National Archives. The list shows overlapping items and whether the National Archives has an original or a copy of the recording.
     </p>
     <p>
      <br/>
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <p>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Selection_criteria">
       Selection criteria
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Selection criteria">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      The criteria for selection are as follows:
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRRC_4-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRRC-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Recordings selected for the National Recording Registry are those that are culturally, historically or aesthetically important, and/or inform or reflect life in the United States.
      </li>
      <li>
       For the purposes of recording selection, "sound recordings" are defined as works that result from the fixation of a series of musical, spoken, or other sounds, but not including the sound component of a moving image work, unless it is available as an autonomous sound recording or is the only extant component of the work.
      </li>
      <li>
       Recordings may be a single item or group of related items; published or unpublished; and may contain music, non-music, spoken word, or broadcast sound.
      </li>
      <li>
       Recordings will not be considered for inclusion into the National Recording Registry if no copy of the recording exists.
      </li>
      <li>
       No recording should be denied inclusion into the National Recording Registry because that recording has already been preserved.
      </li>
      <li>
       No recording is eligible for inclusion into the National Recording Registry until ten years after the recording's creation.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2002">
       2002
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 2002">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      On January 27, 2003, the following 50 selections were announced by the National Recording Preservation Board.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR2_5-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRR2-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3327" data-file-width="2640" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg/100px-Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg/150px-Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg/200px-Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Edison_and_phonograph_edit1.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Selected exhibition recordings for the
        <a href="/wiki/Phonograph" title="Phonograph">
         phonograph
        </a>
        were added in 2002.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1488" data-file-width="1026" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg/100px-BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg/150px-BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg/200px-BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:BookerTWashington-Cheynes.LOC.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Booker_T._Washington" title="Booker T. Washington">
         Booker T. Washington
        </a>
        recreated his controversial 1895 Atlanta Exposition Speech in 1906.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ODJBcard.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="335" data-file-width="545" height="61" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/ODJBcard.JPG/100px-ODJBcard.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/ODJBcard.JPG/150px-ODJBcard.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/ODJBcard.JPG/200px-ODJBcard.JPG 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ODJBcard.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        The
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Original_Dixieland_Jazz_Band" title="Original Dixieland Jazz Band">
         Original Dixieland Jazz Band
        </a>
        's "Tiger Rag" launched
        <a href="/wiki/Jazz" title="Jazz">
         jazz
        </a>
        as a music genre.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bessiesmith.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="996" data-file-width="782" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Bessiesmith.jpg/100px-Bessiesmith.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Bessiesmith.jpg/150px-Bessiesmith.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Bessiesmith.jpg/200px-Bessiesmith.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bessiesmith.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        "
        <a href="/wiki/Downhearted_Blues" title="Downhearted Blues">
         Downhearted Blues
        </a>
        " was the first release by
        <a href="/wiki/Bessie_Smith" title="Bessie Smith">
         Bessie Smith
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2912" data-file-width="3738" height="78" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg/100px-Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg/150px-Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg/200px-Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Louis_Armstrong_restored.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Louis_Armstrong" title="Louis Armstrong">
         Louis Armstrong
        </a>
        was one of American music's most important figures. The preserved sessions, and his solos in particular, set a standard musicians still strive to equal in their beauty and innovation.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR2_5-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR2-5">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          5
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FDRfiresidechat2.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="261" data-file-width="300" height="87" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/FDRfiresidechat2.jpg/100px-FDRfiresidechat2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/FDRfiresidechat2.jpg/150px-FDRfiresidechat2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/FDRfiresidechat2.jpg/200px-FDRfiresidechat2.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FDRfiresidechat2.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">
         Franklin D. Roosevelt
        </a>
        's "Fireside Chats" "redefined the relationship between the president and the American people."
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR2_5-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR2-5">
          <span>

          </span>

        <a href="/wiki/Orson_Welles" title="Orson Welles">
         Orson Welles
        </a>
        ' 1938 "War of the Worlds" radio drama created alarm and panic across the United States.

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2003">
       2003
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2003">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marian_Anderson.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1410" data-file-width="1041" height="135" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Marian_Anderson.jpg/100px-Marian_Anderson.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Marian_Anderson.jpg/150px-Marian_Anderson.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Marian_Anderson.jpg/200px-Marian_Anderson.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marian_Anderson.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        "He's Got the Whole World in His Hands" was one of
        <a href="/wiki/Marian_Anderson" title="Marian Anderson">
         Marian Anderson
        </a>
        's favorite
        <a href="/wiki/Spiritual_(music)" title="Spiritual (music)">
         spirituals
        </a>
        , and she often performed it at the conclusion of her recitals.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR3_7-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR3-7">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          7
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:EllaFitzgerald.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3688" data-file-width="2426" height="152" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/EllaFitzgerald.jpg/100px-EllaFitzgerald.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/EllaFitzgerald.jpg/150px-EllaFitzgerald.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/EllaFitzgerald.jpg/200px-EllaFitzgerald.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:EllaFitzgerald.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        The Cole Porter
        <i>
         Songbook
        </i>
        was the first of
        <a href="/wiki/Ella_Fitzgerald" title="Ella Fitzgerald">
         Ella Fitzgerald
        </a>
        's many anthologies.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1274" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG/100px-Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG/150px-Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG/200px-Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Chuck_Berry_1971.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Berry" title="Chuck Berry">
         Chuck Berry
        </a>
        - widely considered to have "laid the groundwork for not only a rock and roll sound but a rock and roll stance".
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NW_Class_A.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="362" data-file-width="530" height="68" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/NW_Class_A.jpg/100px-NW_Class_A.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/NW_Class_A.jpg/150px-NW_Class_A.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/NW_Class_A.jpg/200px-NW_Class_A.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NW_Class_A.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/O._Winston_Link" title="O. Winston Link">
         O. Winston Link
        </a>
        's recordings of the sounds produced by a variety of locomotive models capture "the unique and now-lost sounds of the engines which united the United States."
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR3_7-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR3-7">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          7
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Beatles_in_America.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2526" data-file-width="3578" height="71" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/The_Beatles_in_America.JPG/100px-The_Beatles_in_America.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/The_Beatles_in_America.JPG/150px-The_Beatles_in_America.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/The_Beatles_in_America.JPG/200px-The_Beatles_in_America.JPG 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Beatles_in_America.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">
         The Beatles
        </a>
        ' album
        <a href="/wiki/Sgt._Pepper%27s_Lonely_Hearts_Club_Band" title="Sgt. Pepper's Lonely Hearts Club Band">
         Sgt. Pepper's Lonely Hearts Club Band
        </a>
        is arguably one of the most important albums in popular music.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marvin_Gaye_(1973).png">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="358" data-file-width="363" height="99" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png/100px-Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png/150px-Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png/200px-Marvin_Gaye_%281973%29.png 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marvin_Gaye_(1973).png" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Marvin_Gaye" title="Marvin Gaye">
         Marvin Gaye
        </a>
        has been covered by artists from
        <a href="/wiki/The_Who" title="The Who">
         The Who
        </a>
        to
        <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Keys" title="Alicia Keys">
         Alicia Keys
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4928" data-file-width="3280" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg/100px-Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg/150px-Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg/200px-Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bruce_Springsteen_-_Roskilde_Festival_2012.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Born_To_Run" title="Born To Run">
         Born To Run
        </a>
        was the breakthrough album for
        <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Springsteen" title="Bruce Springsteen">
         Bruce Springsteen
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

      </sup>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2004">
       2004
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 2004">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      In April 2005, the following 50 selections were made by the National Recording Preservation Board.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR4_8-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRR4-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AdeleFred1921.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="498" data-file-width="600" height="83" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/AdeleFred1921.jpg/100px-AdeleFred1921.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/AdeleFred1921.jpg/150px-AdeleFred1921.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/AdeleFred1921.jpg/200px-AdeleFred1921.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AdeleFred1921.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Traditional_pop_music" title="Traditional pop music">
         traditional pop music
        </a>
        song "Fascinating Rhythm," was sung by Fred and Adele Astaire in
        <i>
         Lady, Be Good
        </i>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_(Crisco_restoration,_with_wings).jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1509" data-file-width="1198" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg/100px-Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg/150px-Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg/200px-Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_%28Crisco_restoration%2C_with_wings%29.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Charles_Lindbergh_and_the_Spirit_of_Saint_Louis_(Crisco_restoration,_with_wings).jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        The NBC's coverage of
        <a href="/wiki/Charles_Lindbergh" title="Charles Lindbergh">
         Colonel Lindbergh
        </a>
        in Washington was an important achievement for the network, and involved reporters in three locations in the city.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MacArthur_Manila.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="572" data-file-width="340" height="168" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MacArthur_Manila.jpg/100px-MacArthur_Manila.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MacArthur_Manila.jpg/150px-MacArthur_Manila.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MacArthur_Manila.jpg/200px-MacArthur_Manila.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MacArthur_Manila.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        In spite of the controversy surrounding
        <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">
         MacArthur
        </a>
        at the time, his farewell speech to congress is noted for its eloquence and effectiveness.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR4_8-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR4-8">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          8
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1150" data-file-width="909" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg/100px-Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg/150px-Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg/200px-Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tom_Lehrer_-_Southern_Campus_1960.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Among those to have claimed musical satirist
        <a href="/wiki/Tom_Lehrer" title="Tom Lehrer">
         Tom Lehrer
        </a>
        as an influence are
        <a href="/wiki/Lenny_Bruce" title="Lenny Bruce">
         Lenny Bruce
        </a>
        and
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weird_Al_Yankovic" title="Weird Al Yankovic">
         Weird Al Yankovic
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4200" data-file-width="3300" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg/100px-Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg/150px-Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg/200px-Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Neil_Armstrong_pose.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        "Houston. Tranquility base here. The Eagle has landed... I'm going to step off the LEM now. That's one small step for man, one giant leap for mankind."
        <a href="/wiki/Neil_Armstrong" title="Neil Armstrong">
         Neil Armstrong
        </a>
        's words upon landing on the moon "have become some of the most recognizable and memorable sentences spoken in United States history."
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR4_8-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-NRR4-8">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          8
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>

      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nirvana_around_1992.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="346" data-file-width="367" height="94" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Nirvana_around_1992.jpg/100px-Nirvana_around_1992.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Nirvana_around_1992.jpg/150px-Nirvana_around_1992.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Nirvana_around_1992.jpg/200px-Nirvana_around_1992.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nirvana_around_1992.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Nirvana_(band)" title="Nirvana (band)">
         Nirvana
        </a>
        are considered one of the modern era's most influential bands, helping popularize
        <a href="/wiki/Alternative_rock" title="Alternative rock">
         alternative rock
        </a>
        .

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2005">
       2005
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2005">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      In April 2006, the following 50 selections were made by the National Recording Preservation Board.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR5_9-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRR5-9">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        9
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="394" data-file-width="317" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg/100px-Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg/150px-Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg/200px-Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Paul_Robeson_1942.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        An athlete, a gentleman and a scholar,
        <a href="/wiki/Paul_Robeson" title="Paul Robeson">
         Robeson
        </a>
        used his diverse talents to pave a successful career as a performer and become active in sociopolitical affairs.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="469" data-file-width="500" height="94" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg/100px-Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg/150px-Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg/200px-Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Count_Basie_in_Rhythm_and_Blues_Revue.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Count_Basie" title="Count Basie">
         Count Basie
        </a>
        , prominent band leader during the
        <a href="/wiki/Big_band" title="Big band">
         big band
        </a>
        era, influenced many musicians of his day.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Archibaldmacleish.jpeg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="413" data-file-width="366" height="113" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Archibaldmacleish.jpeg/100px-Archibaldmacleish.jpeg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Archibaldmacleish.jpeg/150px-Archibaldmacleish.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Archibaldmacleish.jpeg/200px-Archibaldmacleish.jpeg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Archibaldmacleish.jpeg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Archibald_MacLeish" title="Archibald MacLeish">
         Archibald MacLeish
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Librarian_of_Congress" title="Librarian of Congress">
         Librarian of Congress
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">
         Pulitzer Prize
        </a>
        -winning poet.

     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="512" data-file-width="723" height="71" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG/100px-Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG/150px-Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG/200px-Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Proctor_and_Bergman_1976.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Don%27t_Crush_That_Dwarf,_Hand_Me_the_Pliers" title="Don't Crush That Dwarf, Hand Me the Pliers">
         Don't Crush That Dwarf...
        </a>
        was the first comedy album to utilize such production techniques including 16-track recording and Dolby noise reduction.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Stevie_Wonder.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2598" data-file-width="1957" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Stevie_Wonder.jpg/100px-Stevie_Wonder.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Stevie_Wonder.jpg/150px-Stevie_Wonder.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Stevie_Wonder.jpg/200px-Stevie_Wonder.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Stevie_Wonder.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Stevie_Wonder" title="Stevie Wonder">
         Stevie Wonder
        </a>
        has been awarded over 20
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards" title="Grammy Awards">
         Grammy Awards
        </a>
        . His 1976 album
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Songs_in_the_Key_of_Life" title="Songs in the Key of Life">
          Songs in the Key of Life
         </a>
        </i>
        won the Grammy that year for Album of the Year.
       </div>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2006">
       2006
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2006">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      On March 6, 2007, the following 25 selections were made by the National Recording Preservation Board.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRR6_10-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRR6-10">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        10
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="581" data-file-width="431" height="135" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg/100px-Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg/150px-Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg/200px-Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cal_Stewart_with_paper.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Cal Stewart was among the most prolific and popular recording artists of the first 20 years of commercial recording.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2585" data-file-width="2235" height="116" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg/100px-Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg/150px-Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg/200px-Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pete_Seeger_NYWTS.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Pete Seeger adapted a gospel song, "I Shall Overcome", by changing "I" to "We", and it became a civil rights standard.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="287" data-file-width="245" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg/100px-Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg/150px-Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg/200px-Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Stones_ad_1965-2.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/(I_Can%27t_Get_No)_Satisfaction" title="(I Can't Get No) Satisfaction">
         (I Can't Get No) Satisfaction
        </a>
        , The Rolling Stones' first U.S. No. 1 is thought to be one of the greatest rock songs.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2007">
       2007
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2007">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Joefalconmusician.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1391" data-file-width="996" height="140" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Joefalconmusician.jpg/100px-Joefalconmusician.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Joefalconmusician.jpg/150px-Joefalconmusician.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Joefalconmusician.jpg/200px-Joefalconmusician.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Joefalconmusician.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        "Allons  Lafayette" was the best-known recording by Cajun accordionist Joe Falcon.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2716" data-file-width="2171" height="125" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg/100px-Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg/150px-Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg/200px-Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Fiorello_LaGuardia.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Fiorello La Guardia read the comics on WNYC radio during the 1945 newspaper delivery strike.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2339" data-file-width="3507" height="67" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg/100px-T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg/150px-T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg/200px-T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:T-Bone_Walker_1972.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/T-Bone_Walker" title="T-Bone Walker">
         T-Bone Walker
        </a>
        - one of the first electric guitarists.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2999" data-file-width="2389" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg/100px-The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg/150px-The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg/200px-The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Sounds_of_Earth_-_GPN-2000-001976.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <i>
         Murmurs of Earth
        </i>
        is an eclectic 90-minute record of life and culture, sent into space by
        <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">
         NASA
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2008">
       2008
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2008">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4070" data-file-width="2442" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg/100px-Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg/150px-Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg/200px-Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Heifetz_LOC_38890u.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Shortly after his Carnegie Hall debut, violinist
        <a href="/wiki/Jascha_Heifetz" title="Jascha Heifetz">
         Jascha Heifetz
        </a>
        made his first recordings for
        <a href="/wiki/Victor_Talking_Machine_Company" title="Victor Talking Machine Company">
         Victor
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mary_Lou_Williams_(Gottlieb_09231).jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="919" data-file-width="921" height="100" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg/100px-Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg/150px-Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg/200px-Mary_Lou_Williams_%28Gottlieb_09231%29.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mary_Lou_Williams_(Gottlieb_09231).jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Mary_Lou_Williams" title="Mary Lou Williams">
         Mary Lou Williams
        </a>
        was a prolific jazz pianist, composer, and arranger.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3407" data-file-width="2730" height="125" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg/100px-Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg/150px-Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg/200px-Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sir_Winston_S_Churchill.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        Winston Churchill's "
        <a class="extiw" href="//en.wikisource.org/wiki/Sinews_of_Peace" title="s:Sinews of Peace">
         Sinews of Peace
        </a>
        " address originated the term "Iron Curtain."
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" height="75" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg/100px-Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg/150px-Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg/200px-Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Link_Wray_-_3-8-03_Photo_by_Anthony_Pepitone.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        With
        <a href="/wiki/Rumble_(instrumental)" title="Rumble (instrumental)">
         Rumble
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Link_Wray" title="Link Wray">
         Link Wray
        </a>
        invented the
        <a href="/wiki/Power_chord" title="Power chord">
         power chord
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2009">

      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2010">
       2010
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2010">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ishi_portrait.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1282" data-file-width="933" height="137" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Ishi_portrait.jpg/100px-Ishi_portrait.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Ishi_portrait.jpg/150px-Ishi_portrait.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Ishi_portrait.jpg/200px-Ishi_portrait.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ishi_portrait.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Ishi" title="Ishi">
         Ishi
        </a>
        , last surviving member of the Yahi tribe
       </div>
      </div>

       </a>

        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1765" height="57" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg/100px-Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg/150px-Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg/200px-Humpback_stellwagen_edit.jpg 2x" width="100"/>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2011">
       2011
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2011">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      On May 23, 2012, the following 25 selections were made by the National Recording Preservation Board.

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Statistics">
       Statistics
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Statistics">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      As of 2014
      <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">
       <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit">
        [update]
       </a>
      </sup>
      , the oldest recording on the list is
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Edouard-Leon_Scott_de_Martinville" title="Edouard-Leon Scott de Martinville">
       Edouard-Leon Scott de Martinville
      </a>
      's
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Phonautograms" title="Phonautograms">
       Phonautograms
      </a>
      which date back to 1853. The most recent is
      <a href="/wiki/Fanfare_for_the_Uncommon_Woman" title="Fanfare for the Uncommon Woman">
       Fanfare for the Uncommon Woman
      </a>
      by
      <a href="/wiki/Joan_Tower" title="Joan Tower">
       Joan Tower
      </a>
      , performed by the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Colorado_Symphony_Orchestra" title="Colorado Symphony Orchestra">
       Colorado Symphony Orchestra
      </a>
      under the direction of
      <a href="/wiki/Marin_Alsop" title="Marin Alsop">
       Marin Alsop
      </a>
      , which was released in 1999.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRPB2_19-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRPB2-19">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        19
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Selections vary widely in duration. Both the early Edison recordings and the instrumental "
      <a href="/wiki/Rumble_(instrumental)" title="Rumble (instrumental)">
       Rumble
      </a>
      " by
      <a href="/wiki/Link_Wray" title="Link Wray">
       Link Wray
      </a>
      clock in at under three minutes; the
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Edison_Talking_Doll_cylinder&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Edison Talking Doll cylinder (la pagina non esiste)">
       Edison Talking Doll cylinder
      </a>
      is only 17 seconds long. Meanwhile
      <a href="/wiki/Georg_Solti" title="Georg Solti">
       Georg Solti
      </a>
      's recording of
      <a href="/wiki/Richard_Wagner" title="Richard Wagner">
       Wagner
      </a>
      's complete
      <i>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ring_Cycle" title="Ring Cycle">
        Ring Cycle
       </a>
      </i>
      is approximately 15 hours in duration and
      <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Scourby" title="Alexander Scourby">
       Alexander Scourby
      </a>
      's recitation of the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_James_Bible" title="King James Bible">
       King James Bible
      </a>
      is over 80 hours in length.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NRPB2_19-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-NRPB2-19">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        19
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>

      <span class="mw-editsection">

       <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Recording_Registry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Notes">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_firesideA">
        <a href="#ref_firesideA">
         <b>
          <sup>
           A
          </sup>
         </b>
        </a>
       </span>
       The original 25 recordings from July 24, 1933 and July 28, 1934 are preserved at the Roosevelt Library in
       <a href="/wiki/Hyde_Park,_New_York" title="Hyde Park, New York">
        Hyde Park
       </a>
       , New York.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
        <a href="#cite_note-20">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         20
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
